                {

      		});

    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => 
    {
    	(() => 
    	{
    		let map = {}, trace = {};
    
    		document.querySelectorAll('[data-widget]').forEach((element) => 
            {
                let widget = element.dataset.widget;

                let entity = 
    			{
    					
    				item_id: 		element.dataset.id,
    				item_name: 		element.dataset.name,
    				item_list_name: element.dataset.list,
    				item_list_id:	element.dataset.list,
    				item_brand: 	element.dataset.brand,
    				category:		element.dataset.category,
    				price: 			parseFloat(element.dataset.price),
    				index: 			parseFloat(element.dataset.position),
    				currency:		AEC.GA4.currency,
    				quantity: 		1,
    				google_business_vertical: 'retail'
    			};

                Object.assign(entity, entity, AEC.GA4.augmentCategories(entity));

            	let attributes = element.dataset.attributes;
                
            	if (attributes)
    	        {
        	        Object.entries(JSON.parse(attributes)).forEach(([key, value]) => 
        	        {
            	        entity[key] = value;
        	        });
        	    }

        	    if (!map.hasOwnProperty(widget))
        	    {
            	    map[widget] = [];
            	    
            	    map[widget].trace = {};
            	    map[widget].entry = [];
            	    map[widget].item_list_id = '';
            	    map[widget].item_list_name = '';
        	    }

        	    if (!map[widget].trace.hasOwnProperty(element.dataset.id))
        	    {
        	    	map[widget].trace[element.dataset.id] = true;
            	    
            	    map[widget].entry.push(entity);

            	    map[widget].item_list_id 	= entity.item_list_id;
            	    map[widget].item_list_name 	= entity.item_list_name;
        	    } 
            });

    		Object.entries(map).forEach(([key, value]) => 
	        {
		        if (value.entry.length)
		        {
    		        let data = 
    			    {
    					event: 'view_item_list',
    					ecommerce:
    					{
    						item_list_id: 	value.item_list_id,
    						item_list_name: value.item_list_name,
    						items: 			value.entry
    					}
    				};

    		        if ('undefined' !== typeof dataLayer)
    				{
    					(function(callback)
    					{
    						if (AEC.Const.COOKIE_DIRECTIVE)
    						{
    							AEC.CookieConsent.queue(callback).process();
    						}
    						else 
    						{
    							callback.apply(window,[]);
    						}
    					})
    					(
    						(function(dataLayer, data)
    						{
    							return function()
    							{
    								AEC.EventDispatcher.trigger('ec.widget.view.data', data);

    								if (AEC.reset)
    								{
    									dataLayer.push({ ecommerce: null });
    								}
    								
    								dataLayer.push(data);
    							}
    						})(dataLayer, data)
    					);
    				}
		        }
	        });
    	})();
    });

<script>
            // Fix to prevent 'no reCaptcha Token' error while slow site loading.
            // Submit button should catch am-captcha.js initialization8 first
            (function () {
                if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', onReadyStateListener);
                } else {
                    onReadyState();
                }

                function onReadyStateListener() {
                    onReadyState();
                }

                function onReadyState (formsOnPage) {
                    if (typeof formsOnPage === 'undefined') {
                        let formsToProtect = "form\u005Baction\u002A\u003D\u0022customer\u002Faccount\u002Fcreatepost\u0022\u005D,form\u005Baction\u002A\u003D\u0022customer\u002Faccount\u002FloginPost\u0022\u005D,form\u005Baction\u002A\u003D\u0022contact\u002Findex\u002Fpost\u0022\u005D,form\u005Baction\u002A\u003D\u0022customer\u002Faccount\u002Fforgotpasswordpost\u0022\u005D,form\u005Baction\u002A\u003D\u0022review\u002Fproduct\u002Fpost\u0022\u005D,form\u005Baction\u002A\u003D\u0022customer\u002Faccount\u002Fresetpasswordpost\u0022\u005D,form\u005Baction\u002A\u003D\u0022checkout_payment_captcha\u0022\u005D,.form.password.forget";
                        let forms = formsToProtect.split(',');

                        formsOnPage = [];
                        forms.forEach(form => {
                            let existingForm = form ? document.querySelectorAll(form) : [];

                            if (existingForm.length) {
                                formsOnPage.push(existingForm);
                            }
                        })
                    }

                    formsOnPage.forEach(form => {
                        let submit = form[0].querySelector('[type="submit"]');
                        if (submit) {
                            let isAlreadyDisabled = submit.getAttribute('disabled');

                            if (!isAlreadyDisabled) {
                                submit.setAttribute('disabled', true);
                                submit.setAttribute('am-captcha-protect', true);
                            }
                        }
                    })
                }

                            })();
        </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
require(["jquery"],function($){
$('body').on("click",".more, .less",function(){
    var obj = $(this);
    var currentQty = obj.siblings('.cart-item-qty').val();
    var iid = obj.siblings('.update-cart-item').attr('data-cart-item');

    if(obj.hasClass('more')){
        var newAdd = parseInt(currentQty)+parseInt(1);
        obj.siblings('.cart-item-qty').val(newAdd);
        obj.siblings('.cart-item-qty').attr('data-item-qty',newAdd);
        $('#update-cart-item-'+iid).click();
    } else {
        if(parseInt(currentQty) > 1){
            var newAdd = parseInt(currentQty)-parseInt(1);
            obj.siblings('.cart-item-qty').val(newAdd); 
            obj.siblings('.cart-item-qty').attr('data-item-qty',newAdd);
            $('#update-cart-item-'+iid).click();
        }
    }
});
});
</script>

condi\u00e7\u00f5es gerais para efetuar a compra de produtos oferecidos atrav\u00e9s da \u003Ca href=\"https:\/\/mesoestetic.pt\"\u003Ewww.mesoestetic.pt\u003C\/a\u003E e que \r\n        compreende e conte\u00fados que atentem contra os direitos fundamentais e contra as liberdades p\u00fablicas reconhecidos quer constitucionalmente quer nos tratados internacionais ou, simplesmente, que se tornem     require(["jquery"],function($){
        $('.more, .less').on("click",function(){
            var $this = $(this);
            var currentQty = $this.siblings('.input-text').val();

            if($this.hasClass('more')){
                console.log(parseInt(currentQty)+parseInt(1));

<script>
// Obtener el dominio de forma robusta (ignorando puertos)
var host = window.location.hostname;

// Festivos fijos (sin importar el año)
const festivosFijos = [
    "01/01", "06/01", "01/05", "02/05", "15/08",
    "11/09", "12/09", "23/06", "24/06", "24/09",
    "06/12", "08/12", "25/12", "26/12", "29/12",
    "30/12", "31/12"
];

// Festivos variables para 2025
const festivosVariables = [
    "18/04", // Viernes Santo
    "21/04", // Lunes de Pascua
    "09/06"  // Lunes de Pentecostés
];

// Función auxiliar para dos dígitos
function formatoDosDigitos(n) {
    return String(n).padStart(2, '0');
}

// Función global para validar si la fecha es festiva o fin de semana
window.esFestivo = function(fecha = new Date()) {
    const diaSemana = fecha.getDay(); // 0 = domingo, 6 = sábado
    const ddmm = formatoDosDigitos(fecha.getDate()) + '/' + formatoDosDigitos(fecha.getMonth() + 1);
    return festivosFijos.includes(ddmm) || festivosVariables.includes(ddmm) || diaSemana === 0 || diaSemana === 6;
};

// Asignar número de teléfono según dominio
var telephone, flag = false;

switch (host) {
    case "www.mesoestetic.es":
    case "mesoestetic.es":
        telephone = '34659197147';
        flag = true;
        break;
    case "www.mesoestetic.fr":
    case "mesoestetic.fr":
        telephone = '34679904609';
        flag = true;
        break;
    case "www.mesoestetic.pt":
    case "mesoestetic.pt":
        telephone = '34616854454';
        flag = true;
        break;
    // No se define default en producción. Dominios no reconocidos no activan WhatsApp.
}
</script>
<script>
    
    require(['jquery'], function ($) {

        $(".container-contact-button").on("click", function () {
            $('.container-contact-wrapper').toggleClass("active");
            $(this).toggleClass("active");

            showButtonWhatsapp();

            zE('webWidget', 'open');
            zE('webWidget:on', 'chat:status', function(status) {    

                // Verifica si el estado del chat es visible
                if (status === 'online') {
                    $(".link.chat-container").addClass('_show');
                }
                else {
                    $(".link.chat-container").removeClass('_show');
                }
            });
        });

        $(".chat-container").on("click", function () {
            $("#webWidget").show();
            $('.container-contact-wrapper').removeClass("active");
            $('.container-contact-button').removeClass("active");
        });

        // Variables globales definidas en el bloque CMS: telephone, flag, esFestivo()

        function showButtonWhatsapp () {
            const now = new Date;
            const currentTime = now.getTime();

            // Domingo a las 12:00
            const start = new Date(now);
            start.setDate(now.getDate() - now.getDay());
            start.setHours(12, 0, 0, 0);

            // Viernes a las 12:00
            const end = new Date(start);
            end.setDate(start.getDate() + 5);
            end.setHours(12, 0, 0, 0);

            const isFestivity = typeof esFestivo === "function" && esFestivo(now);

            if (currentTime >= start.getTime() && currentTime < end.getTime() && !isFestivity && flag) {
                $(".link.whatsapp-container").addClass('_show');
                $(".link.whatsapp-container").attr('href', "https://api.whatsapp.com/send/?phone=" + telephone);
            }
        }

    });
</script>

                    onload: params.onload,
                    onsave: params.onsave,
                    onupdate: params.onupdate,
                    ondelete: params.ondelete,
                    onerror: params.onerror,
                    oncarouselaction: params.oncarouselaction
                }
            );

            sd.init();

            return sd;
        }
    </script>
<script>
    var clave = "custom-newsletter-popup";
    var valor = "true";
    if(localStorage.getItem(clave) != "true")
    {
        var popup = document.getElementById("popup-suscripcion-nl");

        require(["jquery"], function ($) {

            $(document).ready(function () {

                popup.style.display = "block";
                $( "#popup-suscripcion-nl .popup-close" ).on( "click", function() {
                    $( this ).parent().toggle(false);
                    localStorage.setItem(clave, valor); 
                });

                $( "#popup-suscripcion-nl .btn-unirme" ).on( "click", function() {
                    $( this ).toggle(false);

                    $( "#popup-suscripcion-nl .formulario" ).addClass('active');
                });

            });

        });
    }
</script>
<script>
    require([
        'jquery',
        'tabs',
        'matchMedia',
        'domReady!',
    ], function ($) {
        'use strict';
        var helpers = {
            domReady: function () {
                var $tabs = $('.footer-right');
                mediaCheck({
                    media: '(max-width: 1054px)',
                    entry: function () { // desktop
                        $tabs.find('ul').hide();
                        $tabs.tabs({ active: null, openedState: 'active', collapsible: true })
                    },
                    exit: function () { // mobile
                        $tabs.find('ul').show();
                    }
                });
            },
        }
        helpers.domReady();
    });
</script>
